\DoxyCodeLine{00032\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ Read\ BGLIB\_MSG\_LEN(buffer)\ amount\ of\ bytes\ from\ device\ to\ buffer\ after\ the\ header}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00047\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ \ \ Notes\ about\ SPI\ interface:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00048\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ Byte\ zero\ is\ sent\ by\ module\ when\ there\ is\ no\ valid\ data\ to\ send.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00049\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ Host\ shall\ drop\ bytes\ from\ module\ until\ first\ nonzero\ byte\ is\ received.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00050\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ Host\ shall\ send\ zero\ bytes\ to\ module\ when\ it\ is\ reading\ data\ from\ module}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00051\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ and\ there\ is\ no\ valid\ data\ to\ send.}}
